***uitlopen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitlopen.html>uitlopen</a> (22684)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitlopen.html>uitlopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to walk out</li>
<li>to originate, to arise</li>
<li>to sprout, to <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a></li>
<li>to turn out, to end</li>
<li>to take more time than planned</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">utelôper</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>An offshoot.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sent out.</li></ol>

***uitmaken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitmaken.html>uitmaken</a> (3657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitmaken.html>uitmaken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to matter (only in third-person singular)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>It doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>matter</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitmaken.html>uitmaken</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break up a relationship
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgemaakt.html>uitgemaakt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>She <b><a href = vnd.unilang:broke.html>broke</a> up</b> with <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitmaken.html>uitmaken</a></b>
</p>

***uitmoorden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitmoorden.html>uitmoorden</a> (30202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moorden.html>moorden</a></i>. Attested since the seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitmoorden.html>uitmoorden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exterminate, to annihilate, to murder (almost) all members of a group</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">uitmoording</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitnodigen.html>uitnodigen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to invite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitnodiging.html>uitnodiging</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitnodigingen.html>uitnodigingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitnodiging.html>uitnodigingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>invitation; the act of <span class="Latn" lang="en">inviting</span>; <span class="Latn" lang="en">solicitation</span>, the requesting of a person's company
<ul><li>Dutch Wikipedia, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Linkin_ParkDoorbrak_(2000-2002)" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Linkin Park">Linkin Park</a></span>

<li>A document written or printed, or <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>, conveying the message by which one <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> invited.</li></ol>

***uitscheiden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitscheiden.html>uitscheiden</a> (58839)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheiden.html>scheiden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitscheiden.html>uitscheiden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to secrete</li>
<li>to cease, <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitschieter.html>uitschieter</a> (122309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitschieten.html>uitschieten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitschieter.html>uitschieter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitschieters.html>uitschieters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitschieter.html>uitschietertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***uitslag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitslag.html>uitslag</a> (4142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uteslach</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitslag.html>uitslag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitslagen.html>uitslagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitslag.html>uitslagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">result</span> (e.g. sporting or exam)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">outcome</span> (of a decision)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">rash</span></li>
<li>the act of bringing into circulation</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not protected by dikes</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the act of driving livestock into pastures</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huiduitslag.html>huiduitslag</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koortsuitslag.html>koortsuitslag</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:luieruitslag.html>luieruitslag</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">wedstrijduitslag</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitspreken.html>uitspreken</a> (5638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
